   278	/**
   279	 * Format HPKE Buffer Function
   280	 * Returns a JSON string of an encrypted bundle, separating out the cipher text and the sender public key
   281	 *
   282	 * @param {Uint8Array} encryptedBuf - The result of hpkeAuthEncrypt or hpkeEncrypt
   283	 * @returns {string} - A JSON string with "encappedPublic" and "ciphertext"
   284	 */
   285	
   286	export const formatHpkeBuf = (encryptedBuf: Uint8Array): string => {
   287	  const compressedSenderBuf = encryptedBuf.slice(0, 33);
   288	  const encryptedData = encryptedBuf.slice(33);
   289	
   290	  const encappedKeyBufHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(
   291	    uncompressRawPublicKey(compressedSenderBuf),
   292	  );
   293	  const ciphertextHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(encryptedData);
   294	
   295	  return JSON.stringify({
   296	    encappedPublic: encappedKeyBufHex,
   297	    ciphertext: ciphertextHex,
   298	  });
   299	};
   300	
   301	/**
   302	 * HPKE Decrypt Function
   303	 * Decrypts data using Hybrid Public Key Encryption (HPKE) standard https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9180/.
   304	 *
   305	 * @param {HpkeDecryptParams} params - The decryption parameters including ciphertext, encapsulated key, and receiver private key.
   306	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The decrypted data.
   307	 */
   308	export const hpkeDecrypt = ({
   309	  ciphertextBuf,
   310	  encappedKeyBuf,
   311	  receiverPriv,
   312	}: HpkeDecryptParams): Uint8Array => {
   313	  try {
   314	    let ikm: Uint8Array;
   315	    let info: Uint8Array;
   316	    const receiverPubBuf = getPublicKey(
   317	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverPriv),
   318	      false,
   319	    );
   320	    const aad = buildAdditionalAssociatedData(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPubBuf); // Eventually we want users to be able to pass in aad as optional
   321	
   322	    // Step 1: Generate Shared Secret
   323	    const ss = deriveSS(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPriv);
   324	
   325	    // Step 2: Generate the KEM context
   326	    const kemContext = getKemContext(
   327	      encappedKeyBuf,
   328	      uint8ArrayToHexString(receiverPubBuf),
   329	    );
   330	
   331	    // Step 3: Build the HKDF inputs for key derivation
   332	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, SUITE_ID_1);
   333	    info = buildLabeledInfo(LABEL_SHARED_SECRET, kemContext, SUITE_ID_1, 32);
   334	    const sharedSecret = extractAndExpand(new Uint8Array([]), ikm, info, 32);
   335	
   336	    // Step 4: Derive the AES key
   337	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_SECRET, new Uint8Array([]), SUITE_ID_2);
   338	    info = AES_KEY_INFO;
   339	    const key = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   340	
   341	    // Step 5: Derive the initialization vector
   342	    info = IV_INFO;
   343	    const iv = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   344	
   345	    // Step 6: Decrypt the data using AES-GCM
   346	    const decryptedData = aesGcmDecrypt(ciphertextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   347	    return decryptedData;
   348	  } catch (error) {
   349	    throw new Error(`Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: ${error} `);
   350	  }
   351	};
   352	
   353	/**
   354	 * Generate a P-256 key pair. Contains the hexed privateKey, publicKey, and Uncompressed publicKey
   355	 *
   356	 * @returns {KeyPair} - The generated key pair.
   357	 */
   358	export const generateP256KeyPair = (): KeyPair => {
   359	  const privateKey = randomBytes(32);
   360	  const publicKey = getPublicKey(privateKey, true);
   361	  const publicKeyUncompressed = uint8ArrayToHexString(
   362	    uncompressRawPublicKey(publicKey),
   363	  );
   364	  return {
   365	    privateKey: uint8ArrayToHexString(privateKey),
   366	    publicKey: uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey),
   367	    publicKeyUncompressed,
   368	  };
   369	};
   370	
   371	/**
   372	 * Create additional associated data (AAD) for AES-GCM decryption.
   373	 *
   374	 * @param {Uint8Array} senderPubBuf
   375	 * @param {Uint8Array} receiverPubBuf
   376	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The resulting concatenation of sender and receiver pubkeys.
   377	 */
   378	export const buildAdditionalAssociatedData = (
   379	  senderPubBuf: Uint8Array,
   380	  receiverPubBuf: Uint8Array,
   381	): Uint8Array => {
   382	  return new Uint8Array([
   383	    ...Array.from(senderPubBuf),
   384	    ...Array.from(receiverPubBuf),
   385	  ]);
   386	};
   387	
   388	/**
   389	 * Accepts a private key Uint8Array in the PKCS8 format, and returns the encapsulated private key.
   390	 *
   391	 * @param {Uint8Array} privateKey - A PKCS#8 private key structured with the key data at a specific position. The actual key starts at byte 36 and is 32 bytes long.
   392	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The private key.
   393	 */
   394	export const extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes = (
   395	  privateKey: Uint8Array,
   396	): Uint8Array => {
   397	  return privateKey.slice(36, 36 + 32);
   398	};
   399	
   400	/**
   401	 * Accepts a public key Uint8Array, and returns a Uint8Array with the compressed version of the public key.
   402	 *
   403	 * @param {Uint8Array} rawPublicKey - The raw public key.
   404	 * @return {Uint8Array} – The compressed public key.
   405	 */
   406	export const compressRawPublicKey = (rawPublicKey: Uint8Array): Uint8Array => {
   407	  const len = rawPublicKey.byteLength;
   408	
   409	  // Drop the y coordinate
   410	  // Uncompressed key is in the form 0x04||x||y
   411	  // `len >>> 1` is a more concise way to write `floor(len/2)`
   412	  var compressedBytes = rawPublicKey.slice(0, (1 + len) >>> 1);
   413	
   414	  // Encode the parity of `y` in first bit
   415	  // `BYTE & 0x01` tests for parity and returns 0x00 when even, or 0x01 when odd
   416	  // Then `0x02 | <parity test result>` yields either 0x02 (even case) or 0x03 (odd).
   417	  compressedBytes[0] = 0x02 | (rawPublicKey[len - 1]! & 0x01);
   418	  return compressedBytes;
   419	};
   420	
   421	/**
   422	 * Accepts a public key array buffer, and returns a buffer with the uncompressed version of the public key
   423	 * @param {Uint8Array} rawPublicKey - The public key.
   424	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The uncompressed public key.
   425	 */
   426	export const uncompressRawPublicKey = (
   427	  rawPublicKey: Uint8Array,
   428	  curve: Curve = "CURVE_P256",
   429	): Uint8Array => {
   430	  if (rawPublicKey.length !== 33) {
   431	    throw new Error("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid length");
   432	  }
   433	
   434	  if (!(rawPublicKey[0] === 2 || rawPublicKey[0] === 3)) {
   435	    throw new Error("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid prefix");
   436	  }
   437	
   438	  // point[0] must be 2 (false) or 3 (true).
   439	  // this maps to the initial "02" or "03" prefix
   440	  const lsb = rawPublicKey[0] === 3;
   441	  const x = BigInt("0x" + uint8ArrayToHexString(rawPublicKey.subarray(1)));
   442	
   443	  let p: bigint, a: bigint, b: bigint;
   444	  if (curve === "CURVE_P256") {
   445	    // p-256 domain parameters
   446	    // https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/FIPS/NIST.FIPS.186-4.pdf (Appendix D).
   447	    p = BigInt(
   448	      "115792089210356248762697446949407573530086143415290314195533631308867097853951",
   449	    );
   450	    b = BigInt(
   451	      "0x5ac635d8aa3a93e7b3ebbd55769886bc651d06b0cc53b0f63bce3c3e27d2604b",
   452	    );
   453	    a = p - BigInt(3);
   454	  } else {
   455	    // secp256k1 domain parameters
   456	    // https://www.secg.org/sec2-v2.pdf (Section 2.4.1).
   457	    p = BigInt(
   458	      "0xfffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffefffffc2f",
   459	    );
   460	    a = BigInt(0);
   461	    b = BigInt(7);
   462	  }
   463	
   464	  // Now compute y based on x
   465	  const rhs = ((x * x + a) * x + b) % p;
   466	  let y = modSqrt(rhs, p);
   467	  if (lsb !== testBit(y, 0)) {
   468	    y = (p - y) % p;
   469	  }
   470	
   471	  if (x < BigInt(0) || x >= p) {
   472	    throw new Error("x is out of range");
   473	  }
   474	
   475	  if (y < BigInt(0) || y >= p) {
   476	    throw new Error("y is out of range");
   477	  }
   478	
   479	  var uncompressedHexString = "04" + bigIntToHex(x, 64) + bigIntToHex(y, 64);
   480	  return uint8ArrayFromHexString(uncompressedHexString);
   481	};
   482	
   483	/**
   484	 * Build labeled Initial Key Material (IKM).
   485	 *
   486	 * @param {Uint8Array} label - The label to use.
   487	 * @param {Uint8Array} ikm - The input key material.
   488	 * @param {Uint8Array} suiteId - The suite identifier.
   489	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The labeled IKM.
   490	 */
   491	const buildLabeledIkm = (
   492	  label: Uint8Array,
   493	  ikm: Uint8Array,
   494	  suiteId: Uint8Array,
   495	): Uint8Array => {
   496	  const combinedLength =
   497	    HPKE_VERSION.length + suiteId.length + label.length + ikm.length;
   498	  const ret = new Uint8Array(combinedLength);
   499	  let offset = 0;
   500	
   501	  ret.set(HPKE_VERSION, offset);
   502	  offset += HPKE_VERSION.length;
   503	
   504	  ret.set(suiteId, offset);
   505	  offset += suiteId.length;
   506	
   507	  ret.set(label, offset);
   508	  offset += label.length;
   509	
   510	  ret.set(ikm, offset);
   511	
   512	  return ret;
   513	};
   514	
   515	/**
   516	 * Build labeled info for HKDF operations.
   517	 *
   518	 * @param {Uint8Array} label - The label to use.
   519	 * @param {Uint8Array} info - Additional information.
   520	 * @param {Uint8Array} suiteId - The suite identifier.

   396	        /// <summary>
   397	        /// HPKE-Base mode decrypt (P-256 / HKDF-SHA256 / AES-128-GCM).
   398	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>crypto.ts hpkeDecrypt</c>.
   399	        /// </summary>
   400	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">
   401	        /// Wraps any underlying decryption failure with the upstream
   402	        /// message <c>"Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: ..."</c>.
   403	        /// </exception>
   404	        public static byte[] HpkeDecrypt(HpkeDecryptParams parameters)
   405	        {
   406	            try
   407	            {
   408	                if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   409	                var ciphertextBuf = parameters.CiphertextBuf
   410	                                    ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.CiphertextBuf));
   411	                var encappedKeyBuf = parameters.EncappedKeyBuf
   412	                                     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.EncappedKeyBuf));
   413	                var receiverPriv = parameters.ReceiverPriv
   414	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.ReceiverPriv));
   415	
   416	                var receiverPrivBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverPriv);
   417	                var receiverPubBuf = GetPublicKey(receiverPrivBytes, false);
   418	
   419	                var aad = BuildAdditionalAssociatedData(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPubBuf);
   420	                var ss = DeriveSS(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPriv);
   421	                var kemContext = GetKemContext(encappedKeyBuf, Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(receiverPubBuf));
   422	
   423	                var ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, Constants.SUITE_ID_1);
   424	                var info = BuildLabeledInfo(Constants.LABEL_SHARED_SECRET, kemContext, Constants.SUITE_ID_1, 32);
   425	                var sharedSecret = ExtractAndExpand(Array.Empty<byte>(), ikm, info, 32);
   426	
   427	                ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_SECRET, Array.Empty<byte>(), Constants.SUITE_ID_2);
   428	                info = Constants.AES_KEY_INFO;
   429	                var key = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   430	
   431	                info = Constants.IV_INFO;
   432	                var iv = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   433	
   434	                return AesGcmDecrypt(ciphertextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   435	            }
   436	            catch (Exception error)
   437	            {
   438	                throw new InvalidOperationException(
   439	                    "Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: " + error.Message + " ", error);
   440	            }
   441	        }
   442

   456	        public static byte[] HpkeEncrypt(HpkeEncryptParams parameters)
   457	        {
   458	            try
   459	            {
   460	                if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));

   468	                var senderPubBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   469

   821	                    || !string.Equals(bundleOrgId, parameters.OrganizationId, StringComparison.Ordinal))

   829	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(encappedPublic))

   831	                    throw new InvalidOperationException("missing \"encappedPublic\" in bundle signed data");
   832	                }
   833	                string? ciphertextStr = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "ciphertext");
   834	
   835	                var encappedKeyBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(encappedPublic!);
   836	                var ciphertextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ciphertextStr!);
   837

   839	                {

   846	                    && !parameters.ReturnMnemonic)

   849	                    {
   850	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(

   852	                    }
   853	                    // Derive Ed25519 public key from the 32-byte seed via BouncyCastle.
   854	                    var ed25519PrivKey = new Ed25519PrivateKeyParameters(decryptedData, 0);
   855	                    var publicKeyBytes = ed25519PrivKey.GeneratePublicKey().GetEncoded();

   857	                    {
   858	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(

tests/Fixtures/api-key-stamper/turnkey-api-key-stamper-vectors.json:11:    "note": "P-256 ECDSA signatures are NOT byte-identical across upstream runtimes when the impl uses random-k (nodecrypto.ts, webcrypto.ts). This C# port mirrors upstream's purejs runtime which uses RFC 6979 deterministic-k AND low-S (noble v1.3.0 default), so the C# signature bytes ARE reproducible against an upstream purejs runtime. All three upstream runtimes produce signatures that verify under the same public key + SHA-256(content), so end-to-end Turnkey API calls work regardless of runtime.",
tests/Fixtures/api-key-stamper/turnkey-api-key-stamper-vectors.json:12:    "byte_level_assertion_strategy": "Exact Node-generated byte snapshots would require running the upstream npm package with its full node_modules; the tarball ships only built JS + declarations. Instead, ApiKeyStamperTests asserts wire-format equivalence by: (1) reproducing the upstream stamp-test.ts shape (decoded JSON key order = ['publicKey', 'scheme', 'signature']; scheme constant; publicKey equality); (2) crypto-verifying the DER ECDSA signature against SHA-256(content) under the upstream fixture public key; (3) asserting RFC 6979 determinism (same content -> same signature); (4) asserting low-S (s in (0, n/2]). This combination is sufficient to guarantee the stamp is accepted by Turnkey's backend, which is the wire-format goal."

.github/workflows/release.yml
     1	name: Release
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  release:
     5	    types: [published]
     6	
     7	# Allow re-running the same tag if the prior run failed mid-flight,
     8	# but never two different runs in parallel for the same tag.
     9	concurrency:
    10	  group: release-${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    11	  cancel-in-progress: false
    12	
    13	permissions:
    14	  contents: write       # upload Release assets
    15	  packages: write       # publish to nuget.pkg.github.com
    16	  id-token: write       # attest-build-provenance OIDC
    17	  attestations: write   # attest-build-provenance writes attestations
    18	
    19	jobs:
    20	  publish:
    21	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    22	    env:
    23	      RELEASE_TAG:      ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    24	      GITHUB_ACTOR_ENV: ${{ github.actor }}
    25	
    26	    steps:
    27	      # actions/checkout v6.0.2 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
    28	      - name: Checkout tag
    29	        uses: actions/checkout@de0fac2e4500dabe0009e67214ff5f5447ce83dd
    30	        with:
    31	          ref: ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
    32	          fetch-depth: 0
    33	          # Drop checkout token from .git/config after checkout — later
    34	          # git/gh calls pass `GH_TOKEN` explicitly and never authenticate
    35	          # via the persisted checkout credential, so persisting it
    36	          # extends the token's blast radius without benefit.
    37	          persist-credentials: false
    38	
    39	      - name: Parse + validate strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag
    40	        id: ver
    41	        env:
    42	          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
    43	        run: |
    44	          set -euo pipefail
    45	          # Strict SemVer 2.0.0 (no build metadata): vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]
    46	          # PRERELEASE = identifier (. identifier)*
    47	          # identifier = numeric (no leading zero) | alphanumeric
    48	          re='^v(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)(-((0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*)(\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*))*))?$'
    49	          if [[ ! "$TAG" =~ $re ]]; then
    50	            echo "::error::Tag '$TAG' is not strict SemVer 2.0.0 (vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]; no build metadata)."
    51	            exit 1
    52	          fi
    53	          echo "version=${TAG#v}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    54	          echo "tag=$TAG"          >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    55	
    56	      - name: Resolve tag commit SHA
    57	        id: tagsha
    58	        env:
    59	          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
    60	        run: |
    61	          set -euo pipefail
    62	          echo "sha=$(git rev-parse "${TAG}^{commit}")" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
    63	
    64	      - name: Verify tag commit is contained in main
    65	        env:
    66	          GH_TOKEN:   ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    67	          OWNER_REPO: ${{ github.repository }}
    68	          TAG_SHA:    ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
    69	        run: |
    70	          set -euo pipefail
    71	          # Use the REST compare API instead of `git fetch origin main`.
    72	          # Reason: `actions/checkout` ran with `persist-credentials:
    73	          # false` (security), so the runner's `.git/config` has no
    74	          # credential to authenticate a `git fetch` against this
    75	          # private repo. `gh api` reads `GH_TOKEN` from the env and
    76	          # works against private repos without persisting a git
    77	          # credential.
    78	          #
    79	          # Semantics: GET /repos/{repo}/compare/{base}...{head} returns
    80	          # `status` ∈ {ahead, behind, identical, diverged}, where
    81	          # `base = main` and `head = TAG_SHA`. The tag is reachable
    82	          # from main iff main contains the tag commit, i.e. main has
    83	          # commits the tag does not (status: `behind`) or main and
    84	          # tag point to the same commit (status: `identical`). Any
    85	          # other status (`ahead`, `diverged`) means the tag carries
    86	          # commits not on main and must be rejected.
    87	          STATUS=$(gh api "repos/${OWNER_REPO}/compare/main...${TAG_SHA}" --jq .status)
    88	          case "$STATUS" in
    89	            behind|identical)
    90	              echo "tag ${TAG_SHA} reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS})"
    91	              ;;
    92	            *)
    93	              echo "::error::Tag commit ${TAG_SHA} is not reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS}). Releases must be cut from a commit on main."
    94	              exit 1
    95	              ;;
    96	          esac
    97	
    98	      # actions/setup-dotnet v5.2.0 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
    99	      - name: Setup .NET 8
   100	        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@c2fa09f4bde5ebb9d1777cf28262a3eb3db3ced7
   101	        with:
   102	          dotnet-version: 8.0.x
   103	
   104	      - name: Restore (locked-mode)

   106	
   107	      - name: Build
   108	        env:
   109	          VERSION: ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   110	          TAG_SHA: ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
   111	        run: |
   112	          dotnet build turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-restore \
   113	            /p:Version="$VERSION" \
   114	            /p:PackageVersion="$VERSION" \
   115	            /p:RepositoryCommit="$TAG_SHA" \
   116	            /p:IncludeSymbols=true \
   117	            /p:SymbolPackageFormat=snupkg
   118	
   119	      - name: Test

   122	          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID:      ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID }}
   123	        run: dotnet test turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-build
   124	
   125	      - name: Pack

   128	          TAG_SHA: ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
   129	        run: |

   134	            /p:RepositoryCommit="$TAG_SHA" \

   136	            /p:SymbolPackageFormat=snupkg
   137	
   138	      - name: Validate local .nupkg + .snupkg contents (strict)
   139	        id: pack_artifacts
   140	        env:
   141	          VERSION: ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   142	        run: |
   143	          set -euo pipefail
   144	          NUPKG="./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${VERSION}.nupkg"
   145	          SNUPKG="./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${VERSION}.snupkg"
   146	          test -f "$NUPKG"  || { echo "::error::nupkg missing";  exit 1; }
   147	          test -f "$SNUPKG" || { echo "::error::snupkg missing"; exit 1; }
   148	
   149	          # .nupkg: strict path enumeration + full-line fixed-string match.
   150	          nupkg_paths=$(unzip -Z1 "$NUPKG")
   151	          echo "$nupkg_paths"
   152	          for f in README.md LICENSE NOTICE \
   153	                   lib/netstandard2.1/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.dll \
   154	                   lib/net8.0/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.dll; do
   155	            echo "$nupkg_paths" | grep -Fxq "$f" \
   156	              || { echo "::error::nupkg is missing exact path '$f'"; exit 1; }
   157	          done
   158	
   159	          # .snupkg: must contain .pdb for both TFMs.
   160	          snupkg_paths=$(unzip -Z1 "$SNUPKG")
   161	          echo "$snupkg_paths"
   162	          for f in lib/netstandard2.1/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.pdb \
   163	                   lib/net8.0/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.pdb; do
   164	            echo "$snupkg_paths" | grep -Fxq "$f" \
   165	              || { echo "::error::snupkg is missing exact path '$f'"; exit 1; }
   166	          done
   167	
   168	          NUPKG_SHA256=$(sha256sum  "$NUPKG"  | awk '{print $1}')
   169	          SNUPKG_SHA256=$(sha256sum "$SNUPKG" | awk '{print $1}')
   170	          # Use step outputs (not $GITHUB_ENV) for explicit, unambiguous
   171	          # cross-step data flow. Consumers reference these as
   172	          # steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.<key> wrapped in workflow
   173	          # expression delimiters at the call site (delimiters omitted
   174	          # in this comment so the YAML parser does not interpolate it).
   175	          {
   176	            echo "nupkg_path=$NUPKG"
   177	            echo "snupkg_path=$SNUPKG"
   178	            echo "nupkg_sha256=$NUPKG_SHA256"
   179	            echo "snupkg_sha256=$SNUPKG_SHA256"
   180	          } >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   181	
   182	      - name: Write release-checksums.txt
   183	        id: checksums
   184	        env:
   185	          VERSION:       ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   186	          TAG_SHA:       ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
   187	          NUPKG_SHA256:  ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
   188	          SNUPKG_SHA256: ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_sha256 }}
   189	        run: |
   190	          set -euo pipefail
   191	          CHECKSUMS="./artifacts/release-checksums.txt"
   192	          {
   193	            echo "# release-checksums for KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk ${VERSION}"
   194	            echo "version          = ${VERSION}"
   195	            echo "source_commit    = ${TAG_SHA}"
   196	            echo "nupkg_sha256     = ${NUPKG_SHA256}"
   197	            echo "snupkg_sha256    = ${SNUPKG_SHA256}"
   198	          } > "$CHECKSUMS"
   199	          echo "checksums_path=$CHECKSUMS" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   200	
   201	      - name: Preflight existing Release assets (unconditional)
   202	        id: preflight
   203	        env:
   204	          GH_TOKEN:        ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   205	          TAG:             ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
   206	          VERSION:         ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   207	          NUPKG_SHA256:    ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
   208	          SNUPKG_SHA256:   ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_sha256 }}
   209	          NUPKG_PATH:      ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
   210	          SNUPKG_PATH:     ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_path }}
   211	          CHECKSUMS_PATH:  ${{ steps.checksums.outputs.checksums_path }}
   212	          NUPKG_NAME:      KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.nupkg
   213	          SNUPKG_NAME:     KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.snupkg
   214	        run: |
   215	          set -euo pipefail
   216	          mkdir -p ./_release_assets
   217	          HAS_PRIOR=false
   218	
   219	          # Enumerate assets that actually exist on the Release. We do NOT
   220	          # treat a failed `gh release download` as "asset missing" —
   221	          # that would swallow auth / rate-limit / API errors. Instead
   222	          # query `gh release view` first and download only what is
   223	          # present.
   224	          assets_json=$(gh release view "$TAG" --json assets)
   225	          present() {
   226	            local name="$1"
   227	            jq -e --arg n "$name" '.assets[] | select(.name == $n)' >/dev/null \
   228	              <<< "$assets_json"
   229	          }
   230	
   231	          # If an asset is present, download MUST succeed; failure here
   232	          # is a hard error (closed-fail).
   233	          check_one() {
   234	            local name="$1"
   235	            local sha256="$2"
   236	            if ! present "$name"; then
   237	              echo "preflight: $name absent"
   238	              return 0
   239	            fi
   240	            HAS_PRIOR=true
   241	            if ! gh release download "$TAG" \
   242	                 --pattern "$name" --dir ./_release_assets; then
   243	              echo "::error::Asset '$name' is listed on the Release but download failed."
   244	              exit 1
   245	            fi
   246	            local existing
   247	            existing=$(sha256sum "./_release_assets/$name" | awk '{print $1}')
   248	            if [[ "$existing" != "$sha256" ]]; then
   249	              echo "::error::Existing Release asset $name sha256 ($existing) differs from local ($sha256). Refusing to clobber."
   250	              exit 1
   251	            fi
   252	            echo "preflight: $name byte-equal"
   253	          }
   254	          check_one "$NUPKG_NAME"  "$NUPKG_SHA256"
   255	          check_one "$SNUPKG_NAME" "$SNUPKG_SHA256"
   256	
   257	          # release-checksums.txt: full byte-equality, not hash-line grep.
   258	          if present "release-checksums.txt"; then
   259	            HAS_PRIOR=true
   260	            if ! gh release download "$TAG" \
   261	                 --pattern 'release-checksums.txt' --dir ./_release_assets; then
   262	              echo "::error::release-checksums.txt is listed but download failed."
   263	              exit 1
   264	            fi
   265	            if ! cmp -s "./_release_assets/release-checksums.txt" "$CHECKSUMS_PATH"; then
   266	              echo "::error::Existing Release asset release-checksums.txt differs byte-for-byte from local. Refusing to clobber."
   267	              diff "./_release_assets/release-checksums.txt" "$CHECKSUMS_PATH" || true
   268	              exit 1
   269	            fi
   270	            echo "preflight: release-checksums.txt byte-equal"
   271	          else
   272	            echo "preflight: release-checksums.txt absent"
   273	          fi
   274	
   275	          echo "has_prior_assets=$HAS_PRIOR" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   276	
   277	      - name: Registry-driven duplicate check
   278	        id: registry
   279	        env:
   280	          GH_TOKEN:       ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   281	          GITHUB_ACTOR:   ${{ env.GITHUB_ACTOR_ENV }}
   282	          PACKAGE_LOWER:  kyuzaninc.turnkey.sdk
   283	          VERSION:        ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
   284	          NUPKG_SHA256:   ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
   285	          OWNER:          ${{ github.repository_owner }}
   286	        run: |
   287	          set -euo pipefail
   288	          URL="https://nuget.pkg.github.com/${OWNER}/download/${PACKAGE_LOWER}/${VERSION}/${PACKAGE_LOWER}.${VERSION}.nupkg"
   289	          HTTP_STATUS=$(curl -sL -o ./registry.nupkg -w '%{http_code}' \
   290	            -u "${GITHUB_ACTOR}:${GH_TOKEN}" "$URL")
   291	          case "$HTTP_STATUS" in
   292	            404)
   293	              echo "version not present in registry → new publish"
   294	              echo "is_safe_rerun=false" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   295	              ;;
   296	            200)
   297	              REG_SHA256=$(sha256sum ./registry.nupkg | awk '{print $1}')
   298	              if [[ "$REG_SHA256" == "$NUPKG_SHA256" ]]; then
   299	                echo "version present and bytes match → safe rerun"
   300	                echo "is_safe_rerun=true" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   301	              else
   302	                echo "::error::Registry has version $VERSION with sha256 $REG_SHA256, locally-built nupkg sha256 is $NUPKG_SHA256. Refusing to clobber. Bump to next patch."
   303	                exit 1
   304	              fi
   305	              ;;
   306	            *)
   307	              echo "::error::Unexpected HTTP $HTTP_STATUS while querying registry for version $VERSION."
   308	              exit 1
   309	              ;;
   310	          esac
   311	          rm -f ./registry.nupkg
   312	
   313	      # NOTE: attestation runs BEFORE publish so attestation failures
   314	      # abort before any immutable package is written to the registry.
   315	      # actions/attest-build-provenance v4.1.0 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
   316	      #
   317	      # `if: vars.ENABLE_ATTESTATION == 'true'` makes the step
   318	      # conditional on a repo-level variable. When unset/false the
   319	      # step is skipped and publish proceeds. When set to the string
   320	      # 'true' (Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → Variables),
   321	      # the step runs and a failure here aborts publish (the
   322	      # immutable-write guard is preserved).
   323	      #
   324	      # Rationale: GitHub Artifact Attestations are only available
   325	      # for PRIVATE / internal repos on GitHub Enterprise Cloud.
   326	      # Free / Pro / Team plans get attestations for PUBLIC repos
   327	      # only. KyuzanInc is not on Enterprise Cloud, so this private
   328	      # repo cannot use attestations on the current plan. Until the
   329	      # repo is moved to Enterprise Cloud OR made public, the
   330	      # variable stays unset and publish proceeds without GitHub
   331	      # build provenance. The other defense-in-depth gates (registry
   332	      # byte-invariant, Release-asset preflight, ancestor check,
   333	      # release-checksums.txt) cover the internal-consumption threat
   334	      # model. Build provenance (SLSA v1.0 Build Level 2 by default
   335	      # with `actions/attest-build-provenance`) is most valuable for
   336	      # EXTERNAL consumers of a PUBLIC package — exactly when the
   337	      # variable SHOULD be flipped on. See docs/release-process.md §8.
   338	      - name: Attest build provenance (nupkg + snupkg)
   339	        if: vars.ENABLE_ATTESTATION == 'true'
   340	        uses: actions/attest-build-provenance@a2bbfa25375fe432b6a289bc6b6cd05ecd0c4c32
   341	        with:
   342	          subject-path: |
   343	            ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
   344	            ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_path }}
   345	
   346	      - name: Publish to GitHub Packages (new publish only)
   347	        if: steps.registry.outputs.is_safe_rerun == 'false'
   348	        env:
   349	          GH_PUSH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   350	          NUPKG_PATH:    ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
   351	          OWNER:         ${{ github.repository_owner }}
   352	        run: |
   353	          # `--no-symbols` per Microsoft docs — .snupkg goes to Release
   354	          # assets only. `--skip-duplicate` deliberately omitted: the
   355	          # registry-driven duplicate check already gated this step.
   356	          dotnet nuget push "$NUPKG_PATH" \
   357	            --source "https://nuget.pkg.github.com/${OWNER}/index.json" \
   358	            --api-key "$GH_PUSH_TOKEN" \
   359	            --no-symbols
   360	
   361	      - name: Upload nupkg + snupkg + checksums to GitHub Release
   362	        env:
   363	          GH_TOKEN:         ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   364	          TAG:              ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
   365	          NUPKG_PATH:       ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
   366	          SNUPKG_PATH:      ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_path }}
   367	          CHECKSUMS_PATH:   ${{ steps.checksums.outputs.checksums_path }}
   368	          HAS_PRIOR_ASSETS: ${{ steps.preflight.outputs.has_prior_assets }}
   369	        run: |
   370	          if [[ "$HAS_PRIOR_ASSETS" == "true" ]]; then
   371	            # Preflight proved all prior assets are byte-equal to local;
   372	            # --clobber is safe.
   373	            gh release upload "$TAG" "$NUPKG_PATH" "$SNUPKG_PATH" "$CHECKSUMS_PATH" --clobber
   374	          else
   375	            gh release upload "$TAG" "$NUPKG_PATH" "$SNUPKG_PATH" "$CHECKSUMS_PATH"
   376	          fi
.github/workflows/release-drafter-autolabel.yml
     1	name: Release drafter — autolabel PR
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  pull_request:
     5	    # `edited` is included so title-edit relabeling triggers. The
     6	    # "Strip stale conventional-commit labels" step below runs only on
     7	    # `edited` events and removes stale conventional-commit labels
     8	    # before the autolabeler re-applies based on the current title.
     9	    # `labeled` / `unlabeled` deliberately excluded so manual maintainer
    10	    # label adjustments are not auto-reverted.
    11	    types: [opened, reopened, synchronize, edited]
    12	
    13	permissions:
    14	  contents: read
    15	  pull-requests: write
    16	
    17	jobs:
    18	  autolabel:
    19	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    20	    env:
    21	      GH_TOKEN:  ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    22	      GH_REPO:   ${{ github.repository }}
    23	      PR_NUMBER: ${{ github.event.pull_request.number }}
    24	    steps:
    25	      # release-drafter's autolabeler only ADDs labels; it cannot remove.
    26	      # If the title changes from "fix:" to "feat:", the stale "fix"
    27	      # label would linger and pollute the version-resolver. Strip the
    28	      # conventional-commit set first ONLY on `edited` so unmodified
    29	      # PR events keep their existing labels intact.
    30	      #
    31	      # We use `gh pr edit --remove-label` (NOT `gh label remove`, which
    32	      # would delete the label from the repository entirely). The script
    33	      # first queries which conventional-commit labels are actually
    34	      # attached to this PR, then only calls --remove-label for those.
    35	      # Any `gh` failure aborts.
    36	      - name: Strip stale conventional-commit labels (edited only)
    37	        if: github.event.action == 'edited'
    38	        run: |
    39	          set -euo pipefail
    40	          conventional='breaking feature fix deps docs ci chore'
    41	
    42	          # List labels actually attached to this PR.
    43	          attached=$(gh pr view "$PR_NUMBER" --json labels --jq '.labels[].name')
    44	
    45	          # Intersect conventional ∩ attached; remove only those.
    46	          for label in $conventional; do
    47	            if grep -Fxq "$label" <<< "$attached"; then
    48	              gh pr edit "$PR_NUMBER" --remove-label "$label"
    49	            fi
    50	          done
    51	
    52	      # release-drafter v7.3.0 autolabeler subpath
    53	      - uses: release-drafter/release-drafter/autolabeler@da8b9b696abad2ad997580e49f4c1c2e03cc2bd2
    54	        with:
    55	          config-name: release-drafter.yml
    56	        env:
    57	          GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
.github/workflows/consumer-smoke.yml
     1	name: Consumer install smoke
     2	
     3	# Verifies that a fresh consumer project can install
     4	# KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk@<version> from nuget.pkg.github.com/KyuzanInc
     5	# and exercise the public API surface (Turnkey.Encoding +
     6	# Turnkey.Crypto + Turnkey.ApiKeyStamper).
     7	#
     8	# This is the canonical "consumer in a GitHub Actions job" pattern
     9	# documented in docs/release-process.md §5. The runner-issued
    10	# `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` carries `read:packages` for the same org by
    11	# default, so no PAT is needed.
    12	#
    13	# Two trigger paths:
    14	#
    15	#   1. workflow_dispatch — manual run on demand. The user supplies
    16	#      the package version and TFM through the inputs.
    17	#
    18	#   2. workflow_run — fires automatically whenever the upstream
    19	#      `Release` workflow completes successfully. The version is
    20	#      derived from the upstream tag (workflow_run.head_branch).
    21	#      `workflow_run` always executes the workflow file that exists
    22	#      on the default branch, so the new trigger is inert on feature
    23	#      branches and only activates once merged to `main`.
    24	
    25	run-name: "Consumer smoke (${{ inputs.package_version || github.event.workflow_run.head_branch || 'unknown' }})"
    26	
    27	on:
    28	  workflow_dispatch:
    29	    inputs:
    30	      package_version:
    31	        description: "Version to install (e.g. 0.1.0-alpha.0)"
    32	        required: true
    33	        default: "0.1.0-alpha.0"
    34	      tfm:
    35	        description: "Target framework moniker"
    36	        required: true
    37	        default: "net8.0"
    38	  workflow_run:
    39	    workflows: ["Release"]   # matches release.yml's `name:` field, not the filename
    40	    types: [completed]
    41	
    42	permissions:
    43	  contents: read
    44	  packages: read
    45	
    46	jobs:
    47	  consumer-install:
    48	    # Title falls back to the upstream tag short name on workflow_run
    49	    # so the job card never shows a dangling "Install + use " on
    50	    # auto-runs (where `inputs.package_version` stringifies to '').
    51	    name: "Install + use ${{ inputs.package_version || github.event.workflow_run.head_branch }}"
    52	    # Skip auto-runs that follow a failed/cancelled Release — there's
    53	    # no package to verify in that case. Manual dispatch always runs.
    54	    if: |
    55	      github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' ||
    56	      (github.event_name == 'workflow_run' && github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success')
    57	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    58	    steps:
    59	      # Resolve which package version + TFM this run should install.
    60	      # `workflow_run` events do not populate the `inputs` context
    61	      # (`inputs` is only available for `workflow_dispatch` and
    62	      # `workflow_call` events per GitHub Actions context rules), so
    63	      # this step branches on `github.event_name` and pulls the
    64	      # version from the upstream tag short name for auto-runs. On
    65	      # manual runs it routes the user inputs through unchanged.
    66	      #
    67	      # Outputs:
    68	      #   - steps.resolve.outputs.package_version
    69	      #   - steps.resolve.outputs.tfm
    70	      - name: Resolve install inputs
    71	        id: resolve
    72	        env:
    73	          EVENT_NAME:   ${{ github.event_name }}
    74	          DISPATCH_VER: ${{ inputs.package_version }}
    75	          DISPATCH_TFM: ${{ inputs.tfm }}
    76	          WR_BRANCH:    ${{ github.event.workflow_run.head_branch }}
    77	          WR_EVENT:     ${{ github.event.workflow_run.event }}
    78	        run: |
    79	          set -euo pipefail
    80	          if [[ "$EVENT_NAME" == "workflow_dispatch" ]]; then
    81	            VER="$DISPATCH_VER"
    82	            TFM="$DISPATCH_TFM"
    83	          else
    84	            # workflow_run from `release.yml`. The upstream Release
    85	            # workflow only triggers on `release: published`, so
    86	            # `workflow_run.event` MUST be 'release' and
    87	            # `workflow_run.head_branch` is the tag ref short name
    88	            # (e.g. 'v0.1.0-alpha.0'). Refuse anything else.
    89	            if [[ "$WR_EVENT" != "release" ]]; then
    90	              echo "::error::Unexpected upstream workflow_run.event '$WR_EVENT' (expected 'release'). Refusing to run."
    91	              exit 1
    92	            fi
    93	            # Strict SemVer 2.0.0 with leading 'v' — kept BYTE-FOR-BYTE
    94	            # in sync with the regex in
    95	            # `.github/workflows/release.yml` step "Parse + validate
    96	            # strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag". Any drift here is a bug.
    97	            re='^v(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)(-((0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*)(\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*))*))?$'
    98	            if [[ ! "$WR_BRANCH" =~ $re ]]; then
    99	              echo "::error::workflow_run.head_branch '$WR_BRANCH' is not a strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag; refusing to install."
   100	              exit 1
   101	            fi
   102	            VER="${WR_BRANCH#v}"
   103	            TFM="net8.0"  # default for auto-runs; matrix-able in a later plan
   104	          fi
   105	          echo "package_version=$VER" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   106	          echo "tfm=$TFM"             >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   107	          echo "Resolved: package_version=$VER, tfm=$TFM (source=$EVENT_NAME)"
   108	
   109	      # actions/checkout v6.0.2 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
   110	      # Checkout is only needed so setup-dotnet can find a workspace.
   111	      - name: Checkout (workspace anchor)
   112	        uses: actions/checkout@de0fac2e4500dabe0009e67214ff5f5447ce83dd
   113	        with:
   114	          persist-credentials: false
   115	
   116	      # actions/setup-dotnet v5.2.0 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
   117	      - name: Setup .NET 8
   118	        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@c2fa09f4bde5ebb9d1777cf28262a3eb3db3ced7
   119	        with:
   120	          dotnet-version: 8.0.x
   121	
   122	      - name: Create fresh consumer project
   123	        env:
   124	          TFM: ${{ steps.resolve.outputs.tfm }}
   125	        run: |
   126	          set -euo pipefail
   127	          mkdir -p /tmp/consumer && cd /tmp/consumer
   128	          dotnet new console --framework "$TFM" --name TurnkeySdkConsumer --force
   129	
   130	      - name: Configure GitHub Packages source via dotnet nuget add source
   131	        env:
   132	          GH_ACTOR: ${{ github.actor }}
   133	          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   134	        run: |
   135	          set -euo pipefail
   136	          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
   137	          # Write the source with credentials into a LOCAL NuGet.config.
   138	          # Using `dotnet nuget add source` lets the CLI handle escaping
   139	          # of the URL/username/token. The resulting NuGet.config
   140	          # contains the token in clear text, which is acceptable here
   141	          # because (a) the file lives inside an ephemeral runner only,
   142	          # and (b) `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` is automatically revoked at
   143	          # job end.
   144	          dotnet nuget add source \
   145	            "https://nuget.pkg.github.com/KyuzanInc/index.json" \
   146	            --name kyuzan-github \
   147	            --username "$GH_ACTOR" \
   148	            --password "$GH_TOKEN" \
   149	            --store-password-in-clear-text
   150	
   151	      - name: Install KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk
   152	        env:
   153	          VERSION: ${{ steps.resolve.outputs.package_version }}
   154	        run: |
   155	          set -euo pipefail
   156	          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
   157	          dotnet add package KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk --version "$VERSION"
   158	
   159	      - name: Write sample Program.cs (exercises public API)
   160	        run: |
   161	          set -euo pipefail
   162	          cat > /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer/Program.cs <<'PROGRAM'
   163	          using System;
   164	          using System.Linq;
   165	          using Turnkey;
   166	
   167	          internal static class Program
   168	          {
   169	              private static int Main()
   170	              {
   171	                  Console.WriteLine("=== KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk consumer smoke ===");
   172	
   173	                  // 1. Turnkey.Encoding — hex round-trip
   174	                  byte[] sample = new byte[] { 0xDE, 0xAD, 0xBE, 0xEF, 0x00, 0x11, 0x22, 0x33 };
   175	                  string hex = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(sample);
   176	                  byte[] back = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
   177	                  bool encodingOk = back.SequenceEqual(sample) && hex == "deadbeef00112233";
   178	                  Console.WriteLine($"[1/3] Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString: \"{hex}\" (round-trip ok: {encodingOk})");
   179	                  if (!encodingOk) return 1;
   180	
   181	                  // 2. Turnkey.Crypto — generate a P-256 keypair
   182	                  var keyPair = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   183	                  bool privOk = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(keyPair.PrivateKey) && keyPair.PrivateKey.Length == 64;
   184	                  bool pubOk  = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(keyPair.PublicKey)  && keyPair.PublicKey.Length  == 66;
   185	                  Console.WriteLine($"[2/3] Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair: priv.len={keyPair.PrivateKey.Length}, pub.len={keyPair.PublicKey.Length} (ok: {privOk && pubOk})");
   186	                  if (!privOk || !pubOk) return 2;
   187	
   188	                  // 3. Turnkey.ApiKeyStamper — sign a sample payload
   189	                  var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(keyPair.PublicKey, keyPair.PrivateKey);
   190	                  var stamp = stamper.Stamp("{\"sample\":\"payload\"}");
   191	                  bool stampOk = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(stamp.StampHeaderValue)
   192	                                 && stamp.StampHeaderName == "X-Stamp";
   193	                  Console.WriteLine($"[3/3] ApiKeyStamper.Stamp: header={stamp.StampHeaderName}, value.len={stamp.StampHeaderValue.Length} (ok: {stampOk})");
   194	                  if (!stampOk) return 3;
   195	
   196	                  Console.WriteLine();
   197	                  Console.WriteLine("Consumer install + use of KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk verified end-to-end.");
   198	                  return 0;
   199	              }
   200	          }
   201	          PROGRAM
   202	
   203	      - name: Build + run consumer sample
   204	        run: |
   205	          set -euo pipefail
   206	          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
   207	          dotnet build -c Release
   208	          dotnet run -c Release --no-build
.github/workflows/pr-title-lint.yml
     1	name: PR title lint
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  pull_request:
     5	    types: [opened, reopened, synchronize, edited]
     6	
     7	permissions:
     8	  contents: read
     9	  pull-requests: read
    10	
    11	jobs:
    12	  lint:
    13	    # Job display name must stay in sync with the required-check name
    14	    # documented in docs/release-process.md: the resulting GitHub UI
    15	    # status is "PR title lint / Verify conventional commit title".
    16	    name: Verify conventional commit title
    17	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    18	    env:
    19	      PR_TITLE: ${{ github.event.pull_request.title }}
    20	    steps:
    21	      - name: Verify conventional commit title
    22	        run: |
    23	          set -euo pipefail
    24	          # Structural regex: <type>(<scope>)?!?: <subject>
    25	          # types: feat, fix, deps, docs, ci, chore, refactor, test
    26	          # scope (when present): non-empty
    27	          # subject: at least one char (further checked below for non-whitespace)
    28	          re='^(feat|fix|deps|docs|ci|chore|refactor|test)(\([^)]+\))?!?: (.+)$'
    29	
    30	          # Apply GitHub's workflow-command escape (per
    31	          # https://docs.github.com/en/actions/reference/workflows-and-actions/workflow-commands#example-evaluating-data-from-untrusted-sources)
    32	          # before inserting untrusted PR-title text into an ::error::
    33	          # annotation. Order matters: encode `%` first so other
    34	          # escape sequences are not double-encoded.
    35	          escape() {
    36	            local s="$1"
    37	            s="${s//%/%25}"
    38	            s="${s//$'\r'/%0D}"
    39	            s="${s//$'\n'/%0A}"
    40	            printf '%s' "$s"
    41	          }
    42	          sanitized_raw=$(printf '%s' "$PR_TITLE" | tr -cd '[:print:]\n\r' | head -c 200)
    43	          sanitized=$(escape "$sanitized_raw")
    44	
    45	          if [[ ! "$PR_TITLE" =~ $re ]]; then
    46	            echo "::error::PR title is not conventional (expect: <type>(scope)?!?: <subject>; types: feat|fix|deps|docs|ci|chore|refactor|test). See docs/release-process.md. Got: ${sanitized}"
    47	            exit 1
    48	          fi
    49	          # Subject must contain at least one non-whitespace character.
    50	          subject="${BASH_REMATCH[3]}"
    51	          if ! printf '%s' "$subject" | grep -Eq '[^[:space:]]'; then
    52	            echo "::error::PR title subject is whitespace-only. Got: ${sanitized}"
    53	            exit 1
    54	          fi

.github/workflows/repo-privacy-check.yml
     1	name: Repo privacy check
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  push:
     5	    branches: [main]
     6	  schedule:
     7	    - cron: '0 9 * * 1'   # Mondays 09:00 UTC
     8	
     9	permissions:
    10	  contents: read
    11	
    12	jobs:
    13	  privacy:
    14	    name: Assert repo is PRIVATE
    15	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    16	    steps:
    17	      - name: Verify visibility
    18	        env:
    19	          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    20	        run: |
    21	          set -euo pipefail
    22	          VIS=$(gh repo view "${{ github.repository }}" --json visibility -q .visibility)
    23	          echo "Visibility: $VIS"
    24	          if [[ "$VIS" != "PRIVATE" ]]; then
    25	            echo "::error::Repository visibility must be PRIVATE, got: $VIS"
    26	            exit 1
    27	          fi
.github/workflows/ci.yml
     1	name: CI
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  push:
     5	    branches: [main]
     6	  pull_request:
     7	    branches: [main]
     8	
     9	permissions:
    10	  contents: read
    11	
    12	jobs:
    13	  build-test:
    14	    name: Build + test (ubuntu-latest, net8.0 runner)
    15	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    16	    steps:
    17	      - uses: actions/checkout@v6
    18	
    19	      - name: Setup .NET 8
    20	        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@v5
    21	        with:
    22	          dotnet-version: 8.0.x
    23	
    24	      - name: Verify packages.lock.json is present
    25	        run: |
    26	          test -f src/packages.lock.json   || (echo "src/packages.lock.json missing"   && exit 1)
    27	          test -f tests/packages.lock.json || (echo "tests/packages.lock.json missing" && exit 1)
    28	
    29	      - name: Restore (locked-mode)
    30	        run: dotnet restore turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln --locked-mode
    31	
    32	      - name: Build (Release, both TFMs)
    33	        run: dotnet build turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-restore
    34	
    35	      - name: Test (Release, with coverage)
    36	        env:
    37	          # E2E tests skip themselves if these are unset
    38	          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY }}
    39	          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID: ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID }}
    40	        run: |
    41	          dotnet test turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-build \
    42	            --collect:"XPlat Code Coverage" \
    43	            --results-directory ./TestResults \
    44	            --logger "trx;LogFileName=test-results.trx"
    45	
    46	      # Coverage gate. Threshold is set to 30% combined-TFM for
    47	      # v0.1.0-alpha because the report counts both the netstandard2.1
    48	      # and net8.0 production assemblies (tests only target net8.0) AND
    49	      # the System.Text.Json source-generated TypeInfo classes (most of
    50	      # which are never executed by tests). The local single-TFM
    51	      # net8.0-only figure is ~78% line.
    52	      # TODOs to raise back:
    53	      #   1. Filter the cobertura output to net8.0 only (or unify reports).
    54	      #   2. Add targeted negative tests for
    55	      #      Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle / EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle /
    56	      #      DecryptExportBundle error paths once Turnkey sample bundles
    57	      #      are committable.
    58	      - name: Coverage gate (>=30% combined-TFM line for v0.1.0-alpha)
    59	        uses: irongut/CodeCoverageSummary@v1.3.0
    60	        with:
    61	          filename: TestResults/**/coverage.cobertura.xml
    62	          badge: false
    63	          fail_below_min: true
    64	          thresholds: '30 50'
    65	          format: markdown
    66	          output: both
    67	
    68	      - name: Upload coverage artifact
    69	        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v7
    70	        if: always()
    71	        with:
    72	          name: coverage-report
    73	          path: TestResults/**
    74	
    75	  pack:
    76	    name: dotnet pack (validation)
    77	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    78	    needs: build-test
    79	    steps:
    80	      - uses: actions/checkout@v6
    81	      - uses: actions/setup-dotnet@v5
    82	        with:
    83	          dotnet-version: 8.0.x
    84	      - name: Restore (locked-mode)
    85	        run: dotnet restore turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln --locked-mode
    86	      - name: Pack (Release)
    87	        run: |
    88	          dotnet pack src/turnkey-sdk-csharp.csproj -c Release \
    89	            --no-restore --output ./artifacts
    90	      - name: Validate NuGet contents (README, LICENSE, NOTICE)
    91	        run: |
    92	          set -euo pipefail
    93	          NUPKG=$(ls ./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.*.nupkg | head -1)
    94	          echo "Validating $NUPKG"
    95	          unzip -l "$NUPKG" | tee /tmp/contents.txt
    96	          grep -q 'README.md' /tmp/contents.txt
    97	          grep -q 'LICENSE'   /tmp/contents.txt
    98	          grep -q 'NOTICE'    /tmp/contents.txt
    99	      - name: Upload .nupkg + .snupkg artifacts
   100	        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v7
   101	        with:
   102	          name: nupkgs
   103	          path: ./artifacts/**

    10	import { generateKeyPairWithOpenSsl } from "./shared";
    11	
    12	beforeAll(() => {
    13	  // @ts-expect-error -- polyfilling the runtime for "webcrypto" and "universal"
    14	  globalThis.crypto = crypto.webcrypto;
    15	});
    16	
    17	test.each([
    18	  { impl: signNode, name: "sign (node crypto)" },
    19	  { impl: signWeb, name: "sign (WebCrypto)" },
    20	  { impl: signPureJS, name: "sign (PureJS)" },
    21	  { impl: signUniversal, name: "sign (universal)" },
    22	])("sign with Turnkey fixture: $name", async ({ impl: sign }) => {
    23	  const { privateKey, publicKey, pemPublicKey } = await readFixture();
    24	
    25	  const content = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString("hex");
    26	
    27	  const signature = await sign({
    28	    content,
    29	    privateKey,
    30	    publicKey,
    31	  });
    32	
    33	  // We can't snapshot `actualStamp.signature` because P-256 signatures are not deterministic
    34	  expect(
    35	    assertValidSignature({
    36	      content,
    37	      pemPublicKey,
    38	      signature: signature,
    39	    }),
    40	  ).toBe(true);
    41	
    42	  // Sanity check
    43	  expect(() => {
    44	    assertValidSignature({
    45	      content: "something else that wasn't stamped",
    46	      pemPublicKey,
    47	      signature: signature,
    48	    });
    49	  }).toThrow();
    50	});
    51	
    52	test.each([
    53	  { impl: signNode, name: "stamp (node)" },
    54	  { impl: signWeb, name: "stamp (WebCrypto)" },
    55	  { impl: signUniversal, name: "stamp (universal)" },
    56	])("sign with openssl generated key pairs: $name", async ({ impl: stamp }) => {
    57	  // Run 20 times, where each run spawns 10 keys in parallel -> 200 tests in total
    58	  for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
    59	    await Promise.all(
    60	      Array.from({ length: 10 }, () => true).map(async () => {
    61	        const { privateKey, publicKey, pemPublicKey } =
    62	          await generateKeyPairWithOpenSsl();
    63	
    64	        // A string of random unicode characters
    65	        const content = Array.from({ length: 64 }, () => {
    66	          return String.fromCharCode(Math.floor(Math.random() * 65536));
    67	        }).join("");
    68	
    69	        const signature = await stamp({
    70	          content,
    71	          privateKey,
    72	          publicKey,
    73	        });
    74	
    75	        // We can't snapshot `actualStamp.signature` because P-256 signatures are not deterministic
    76	        expect(
    77	          assertValidSignature({
    78	            content,
    79	            pemPublicKey,
    80	            signature: signature,
    81	          }),
    82	        ).toBe(true);
    83	
    84	        // Sanity check
    85	        expect(() => {
    86	          assertValidSignature({
    87	            content: "something else that wasn't stamped",
    88	            pemPublicKey,
    89	            signature: signature,
    90	          });
    91	        }).toThrow();
    92	      }),
    93	    );
    94	  }
    95	});

    20	    "0400d2eb47be2006c29db5fe9941dd686d19ddeea85a0328894f08091f6b5be9b366c4872345594c12a7f7c47c62dd8074542934820fce5ee0ddc55d6d1d8dd312";

    22	  expect(jwk.x).toBeDefined();

    28	  let xHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(xBytes);

    31	  // Convert y value to make sure it's the same as second half of uncompressed key

    33	  let yBytes = new Uint8Array(base64urlToBuffer(yString));
    34	  let yHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(yBytes);
    35	  expect(yHex).toBe(uncompPubKey.substring(66, 130));

    40	  const uncompPubKey =
    41	    "0400d2eb47be2006c29db5fe9941dd686d19ddeea85a0328894f08091f6b5be9b366c4872345594c12a7f7c47c62dd8074542934820fce5ee0ddc55d6d1d8dd312";

    47	  expect(jwk.x).toBeDefined();
    48	  expect(jwk.y).toBeDefined();

    51	  let xString: string = jwk.x !== undefined ? jwk.x : "_";
    52	  let xBytes = new Uint8Array(base64urlToBuffer(xString));
    53	  let xHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(xBytes);
    54	  expect(xHex).toBe(uncompPubKey.substring(2, 66));
    55	
    56	  // Convert y value to make sure it's the same as second half of uncompressed key
    57	  let yString: string = jwk.y !== undefined ? jwk.y : "_";
    58	  let yBytes = new Uint8Array(base64urlToBuffer(yString));
    59	  let yHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(yBytes);
    60	  expect(yHex).toBe(uncompPubKey.substring(66, 130));
    61	});
    62	
    63	// Convert base64 url encoded string to an array -- used here to test that output pads correctly and doesn't get truncated
    64	function base64urlToBuffer(baseurl64String: string): ArrayBuffer {
    65	  // Base64url to Base64
    66	  const padding = "==".slice(0, (4 - (baseurl64String.length % 4)) % 4);
    67	  const base64String =
    68	    baseurl64String.replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/") + padding;
    69	
    70	  // Base64 to binary string
    71	  const str = atob(base64String);
    72	
    73	  // Binary string to buffer
    74	  const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(str.length);
    75	  const byteView = new Uint8Array(buffer);
    76	  for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
    77	    byteView[i] = str.charCodeAt(i);
    78	  }
    79	  return buffer;
    80	}

     1	import {
     2	  uint8ArrayFromHexString,
     3	  uint8ArrayToHexString,
     4	} from "@turnkey/encoding";
     5	import type { v1AppProof, v1BootProof } from "@turnkey/sdk-types";
     6	import { p256 } from "@noble/curves/p256";
     7	import { sha256 } from "@noble/hashes/sha2";
     8	import * as CBOR from "cbor-js";
     9	import * as x509 from "@peculiar/x509";
    10	import { AWS_ROOT_CERT_PEM, AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256 } from "./constants";
    11	
    12	export const getCryptoInstance = async () => {
    13	  let cryptoInstance: Crypto;
    14	  // Use globalThis.crypto.subtle if available
    15	  if (typeof globalThis !== "undefined" && globalThis.crypto?.subtle) {
    16	    cryptoInstance = globalThis.crypto as Crypto;
    17	    x509.cryptoProvider.set(cryptoInstance);
    18	
    19	    return cryptoInstance;
    20	  } else {
    21	    throw new Error(
    22	      "Web Crypto API is not available in this environment. You may need to polyfill it.",
    23	    );
    24	  }
    25	};
    26	
    27	/**
    28	 * Utility: SHA-256 digest → hex (uppercase)
    29	 */
    30	async function sha256Hex(data: Uint8Array): Promise<string> {
    31	  const cryptoInstance = await getCryptoInstance();
    32	  const digest = await cryptoInstance.subtle.digest("SHA-256", data);
    33	  return uint8ArrayToHexString(new Uint8Array(digest)).toUpperCase();
    34	}
    35	
    36	/**
    37	 * Utility: Import SPKI public key for ECDSA verify
    38	 */
    39	async function importEcdsaPublicKey(spki: ArrayBuffer): Promise<CryptoKey> {
    40	  const cryptoInstance = await getCryptoInstance();
    41	  return cryptoInstance.subtle.importKey(
    42	    "spki",
    43	    spki,
    44	    { name: "ECDSA", namedCurve: "P-384" }, // AWS Nitro uses ES384
    45	    false,
    46	    ["verify"],
    47	  );
    48	}
    49	
    50	/**
    51	 * verify goes through the following verification steps for an app proof & boot proof pair:
    52	 *  - Verify app proof signature
    53	 *  - Verify the boot proof
    54	 *    - Attestation doc was signed by AWS
    55	 *    - Attestation doc's `user_data` is the hash of the qos manifest
    56	 *  - Verify the connection between the app proof & boot proof i.e. that the ephemeral keys match
    57	 *
    58	 *  For more information, check out https://whitepaper.turnkey.com/foundations
    59	 */
    60	export async function verify(
    61	  appProof: v1AppProof,
    62	  bootProof: v1BootProof,
    63	): Promise<void> {
    64	  // 1. Verify App Proof
    65	  verifyAppProofSignature(appProof);
    66	
    67	  // 2. Verify Boot Proof
    68	  // Parse attestation
    69	  const coseSign1Der = Uint8Array.from(
    70	    atob(bootProof.awsAttestationDocB64)
    71	      .split("")
    72	      .map((c) => c.charCodeAt(0)),
    73	  );
    74	  const coseSign1 = CBOR.decode(coseSign1Der.buffer);
    75	  const [, , payload] = coseSign1;
    76	  const attestationDoc = CBOR.decode(new Uint8Array(payload).buffer);
    77	
    78	  // Verify cose sign1 signature
    79	  await verifyCoseSign1Sig(coseSign1, attestationDoc.certificate);
    80	
    81	  // Verify certificate chain
    82	  const appProofTimestampMs = parseInt(
    83	    JSON.parse(appProof.proofPayload).timestampMs,
    84	  );
    85	  await verifyCertificateChain(
    86	    attestationDoc.cabundle,
    87	    AWS_ROOT_CERT_PEM,
    88	    attestationDoc.certificate,
    89	    appProofTimestampMs,
    90	  );
    91	
    92	  // Verify manifest digest
    93	  const decodedBootProofManifest = Uint8Array.from(
    94	    atob(bootProof.qosManifestB64)
    95	      .split("")
    96	      .map((c) => c.charCodeAt(0)),
    97	  );
    98	  const manifestDigest = sha256(decodedBootProofManifest);
    99	  if (!bytesEq(manifestDigest, attestationDoc.user_data)) {
   100	    throw new Error(
   101	      `attestationDoc's user_data doesn't match the hash of the manifest. attestationDoc.user_data: ${attestationDoc.user_data} , manifest digest: ${manifestDigest}`,
   102	    );
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  // 3. Verify that all the ephemeral public keys match: app proof, boot proof structure, actual attestation doc
   106	  const publicKeyBytes = new Uint8Array(attestationDoc.public_key);
   107	  const attestationPubKey = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKeyBytes);
   108	  if (
   109	    appProof.publicKey !== attestationPubKey ||
   110	    attestationPubKey !== bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex
   111	  ) {
   112	    throw new Error(
   113	      `Ephemeral pub keys from app proof: ${appProof.publicKey}, boot proof structure ${bootProof.ephemeralPublicKeyHex}, and attestation doc ${attestationPubKey} should all match`,
   114	    );
   115	  }
   116	}
   117	
   118	/**
   119	 * Verify app proof signature with @noble/curves
   120	 */
   121	export function verifyAppProofSignature(appProof: v1AppProof): void {
   122	  if (appProof.scheme !== "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_EPHEMERAL_KEY_P256") {
   123	    throw new Error("Unsupported signature scheme");
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  // Decode public key
   127	  let publicKeyBytes: Uint8Array;
   128	  try {
   129	    publicKeyBytes = uint8ArrayFromHexString(appProof.publicKey);
   130	  } catch {
   131	    throw new Error("Failed to decode public key");
   132	  }
   133	
   134	  if (publicKeyBytes.length !== 130) {
   135	    throw new Error(
   136	      `Expected 130 bytes (encryption + signing pub keys), got ${publicKeyBytes.length} bytes`,
   137	    );
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  // Extract signing key (last 65 bytes, uncompressed P-256 point)
   141	  const signingKeyBytes = publicKeyBytes.slice(65);
   142	  if (signingKeyBytes.length !== 65 || signingKeyBytes[0] !== 0x04) {
   143	    throw new Error(
   144	      "Invalid signing key format: expected 65-byte uncompressed P-256 point (0x04||X||Y)",
   145	    );
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  // Validate it's a valid P-256 public key by attempting to create a point
   149	  try {
   150	    p256.ProjectivePoint.fromHex(signingKeyBytes);
   151	  } catch (error) {
   152	    throw new Error(`Invalid P-256 public key: ${error}`);
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  // Decode signature (64 bytes = 32 bytes r + 32 bytes s)
   156	  let signatureBytes: Uint8Array;
   157	  try {
   158	    signatureBytes = uint8ArrayFromHexString(appProof.signature);
   159	  } catch {
   160	    throw new Error("Failed to decode signature");
   161	  }
   162	  if (signatureBytes.length !== 64) {
   163	    throw new Error(
   164	      `Expected 64 bytes signature (r||s), got ${signatureBytes.length} bytes`,
   165	    );
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  // Hash the proof payload
   169	  const payloadBytes = new TextEncoder().encode(appProof.proofPayload);
   170	  const payloadDigest = sha256(payloadBytes);
   171	
   172	  // Verify ECDSA signature
   173	  const isValid = p256.verify(signatureBytes, payloadDigest, signingKeyBytes);
   174	  if (!isValid) {
   175	    throw new Error("Signature verification failed");
   176	  }
   177	}
   178	
   179	export async function verifyCertificateChain(
   180	  cabundle: Uint8Array[],
   181	  rootCertPem: string,
   182	  leafCert: Uint8Array,
   183	  timestampMs: number,
   184	): Promise<void> {
   185	  try {
   186	    // Check root and assert fingerprint
   187	    const rootX509 = new x509.X509Certificate(rootCertPem);
   188	    const rootDer = new Uint8Array(rootX509.rawData);
   189	    const rootSha = await sha256Hex(rootDer);
   190	    if (rootSha !== AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256) {
   191	      throw new Error(
   192	        `Pinned AWS root fingerprint mismatch: expected=${AWS_ROOT_CERT_SHA256} actual=${rootSha}`,
   193	      );
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    // Bundle starts with root certificate. We're replacing the root with our hardcoded known certificate, so remove first element
   197	    const bundleWithoutRoot = cabundle.slice(1);
   198	    const intermediatesX509 = bundleWithoutRoot.map((c) => {
   199	      if (!c) throw new Error("Invalid certificate data in cabundle");
   200	      return new x509.X509Certificate(c);
   201	    });
   202	    const leaf = new x509.X509Certificate(leafCert);
   203	
   204	    // Build path leaf → intermediates → root, with our hardcoded known root certificate
   205	    const builder = new x509.X509ChainBuilder({
   206	      certificates: [rootX509, ...intermediatesX509],
   207	    });
   208	    const chain = await builder.build(leaf);
   209	    if (chain.length !== intermediatesX509.length + 2) {
   210	      throw new Error(

exec

    64	/**
    65	 * Decrypt an encrypted email auth/recovery or oauth credential bundle.
    66	 *
    67	 * @param {string} credentialBundle - The encrypted credential bundle.
    68	 * @param {string} embeddedKey - The private key for decryption.
    69	 * @returns {string} - The decrypted data or null if decryption fails.
    70	 * @throws {Error} - If unable to decrypt the credential bundle
    71	 */
    72	export const decryptCredentialBundle = (
    73	  credentialBundle: string,
    74	  embeddedKey: string,
    75	): string => {
    76	  try {
    77	    const bundleBytes = bs58check.decode(credentialBundle);
    78	    if (bundleBytes.byteLength <= 33) {
    79	      throw new Error(
    80	        `Bundle size ${bundleBytes.byteLength} is too low. Expecting a compressed public key (33 bytes) and an encrypted credential.`,
    81	      );
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    const compressedEncappedKeyBuf = bundleBytes.slice(0, 33);
    85	    const ciphertextBuf = bundleBytes.slice(33);
    86	    const encappedKeyBuf = uncompressRawPublicKey(compressedEncappedKeyBuf);
    87	    const decryptedData = hpkeDecrypt({
    88	      ciphertextBuf,
    89	      encappedKeyBuf,
    90	      receiverPriv: embeddedKey,
    91	    });
    92	
    93	    return uint8ArrayToHexString(decryptedData);
    94	  } catch (error) {
    95	    throw new Error(`"Error decrypting bundle:", ${error}`);
    96	  }
    97	};
    98	
    99	/**
   100	 * Decrypt an encrypted export bundle (such as a private key or wallet account bundle).
   101	 *
   102	 * This function verifies the enclave signature to ensure the authenticity of the encrypted data.
   103	 * It uses HPKE (Hybrid Public Key Encryption) to decrypt the contents of the bundle and returns
   104	 * either the decrypted mnemonic or the decrypted data in hexadecimal format, based on the
   105	 * `returnMnemonic` flag.
   106	 *
   107	 * @param {DecryptExportBundleParams} params - An object containing the following properties:
   108	 *   - exportBundle {string}: The encrypted export bundle in JSON format.
   109	 *   - organizationId {string}: The expected organization ID to verify against the signed data.
   110	 *   - embeddedKey {string}: The private key used for decrypting the data.
   111	 *   - dangerouslyOverrideSignerPublicKey {string} [Optional]: Optionally override the default signer public key used for verifying the signature. This should only be done for testing
   112	 *   - returnMnemonic {boolean}: If true, returns the decrypted data as a mnemonic string; otherwise, returns it in hexadecimal format.
   113	 * @returns {Promise<string>} - A promise that resolves to the decrypted mnemonic or decrypted hexadecimal data.
   114	 * @throws {Error} - If decryption or signature verification fails, throws an error with details.
   115	 */
   116	export const decryptExportBundle = async ({
   117	  exportBundle,
   118	  embeddedKey,
   119	  organizationId,
   120	  dangerouslyOverrideSignerPublicKey,
   121	  keyFormat,
   122	  returnMnemonic,
   123	}: DecryptExportBundleParams): Promise<string> => {
   124	  try {
   125	    const parsedExportBundle = JSON.parse(exportBundle);
   126	    const verified = await verifyEnclaveSignature(
   127	      parsedExportBundle.enclaveQuorumPublic,
   128	      parsedExportBundle.dataSignature,
   129	      parsedExportBundle.data,
   130	      dangerouslyOverrideSignerPublicKey,
   131	    );
   132	    if (!verified) {
   133	      throw new Error(
   134	        `failed to verify enclave signature: ${parsedExportBundle}`,
   135	      );
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    const signedData = JSON.parse(
   139	      new TextDecoder().decode(
   140	        uint8ArrayFromHexString(parsedExportBundle.data),
   141	      ),
   142	    );
   143	
   144	    if (
   145	      !signedData.organizationId ||
   146	      signedData.organizationId !== organizationId
   147	    ) {
   148	      throw new Error(
   149	        `organization id does not match expected value. Expected: ${organizationId}. Found: ${signedData.organizationId}.`,
   150	      );
   151	    }
   152	    if (!signedData.encappedPublic) {
   153	      throw new Error('missing "encappedPublic" in bundle signed data');
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    const encappedKeyBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(signedData.encappedPublic);
   157	    const ciphertextBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(signedData.ciphertext);
   158	    const decryptedData = hpkeDecrypt({
   159	      ciphertextBuf,
   160	      encappedKeyBuf,
   161	      receiverPriv: embeddedKey,
   162	    });
   163	
   164	    if (keyFormat === "SOLANA" && !returnMnemonic) {
   165	      if (decryptedData.length !== 32) {
   166	        throw new Error(
   167	          `invalid private key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got ${decryptedData.length}.`,
   168	        );
   169	      }
   170	      const publicKeyBytes = ed25519.getPublicKey(decryptedData);
   171	      if (publicKeyBytes.length !== 32) {
   172	        throw new Error(
   173	          `invalid public key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got ${publicKeyBytes.length}.`,
   174	        );
   175	      }
   176	      const concatenatedBytes = new Uint8Array(64);
   177	      concatenatedBytes.set(decryptedData, 0);
   178	      concatenatedBytes.set(publicKeyBytes, 32);
   179	      return bs58.encode(concatenatedBytes);
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    const decryptedDataHex = uint8ArrayToHexString(decryptedData);
   183	    return returnMnemonic ? hexToAscii(decryptedDataHex) : decryptedDataHex;
   184	  } catch (error) {
   185	    throw new Error(`Error decrypting bundle: ${error}`);
   186	  }
   187	};
   188	
   189	/**

   191	 *
   192	 * @param {string} publicKey - The public key of the authenticator (e.g. WebAuthn or P256 API key).
   193	 * @param {string} signature - The ECDSA signature in DER format.
   194	 * @param {string} signedData - The data that was signed (e.g. JSON-stringified Turnkey request body).
   195	 * @returns {Promise<boolean>} - Returns true if the signature is valid, otherwise throws an error.
   196	 *

   206	export const verifyStampSignature = async (

   480	/**
   481	 * Encrypts a message to an uncompressed P256 public key
   482	 * The function takes in standard strings and converts them
   483	 * to Uint8Arrays to be used by the lower level quorumKeyEncrypt
   484	 * function. More details about how the encryption works is described
   485	 * in that function's documentation.
   486	 *
   487	 * @param targetPublicKeyUncompressed A hex string uncompressed public key to encrypt a message to
   488	 * @param message A standard string message to encrypt, does not have to be hex encoded
   489	 * @returns {Promise<Uint8Array>} A borsh serialized envelope with the encrypted message (more details found in quorumKeyEncrypt)
   490	 */
   491	export const encryptToEnclave = async (
   492	  targetPublicKeyUncompressed: string,
   493	  message: string,
   494	): Promise<Uint8Array> => {
   495	  return await quorumKeyEncrypt(
   496	    uint8ArrayFromHexString(targetPublicKeyUncompressed),
   497	    new TextEncoder().encode(message),
   498	  );
   499	};

   501	/**
   502	 * Helper function used specifically to encrypt a client secret to
   503	 * TLS Fetchers quorum key. This is used for client_secret upload
   504	 * when enabling authentication with an OAuth 2.0 provider
   505	 *
   506	 * @param client_secret The client secret issued by the OAuth 2.0 provider
   507	 * @param dangerouslyOverrideTlsFetcherPublicKey *(optional)* Hex-encoded
   508	 *              uncompressed P-256 public key to encrypt to (use only in
   509	 *              tests/dev environment).  Defaults to the production TLS Fetcher key.
   510	 * @returns {Promise<string>} A hex encoded borsh serialized envelope with the encrypted client
   511	 *                            secret meant to be passed to the CreateOauth2Credential Activity
   512	 */
   513	export const encryptOauth2ClientSecret = async (
   514	  client_secret: string,
   515	  dangerouslyOverrideTlsFetcherPublicKey?: string,
   516	): Promise<string> => {

   518	    await encryptToEnclave(
   519	      dangerouslyOverrideTlsFetcherPublicKey ??
   520	        PRODUCTION_TLS_FETCHER_ENCRYPT_PUBLIC_KEY,
   521	      client_secret,
   522	    ),
   523	  );
   524	};

   526	/**
   527	 * Helper function used specifically to encrypt your on ramp private/secret api keys
   528	 * to the on ramp encryption public key. This is used before uploading your on ramp
   529	 * credentials to Turnkey via the CreateFiatOnRampCredential activity
   530	 *
   531	 * @param secret The private/secret api key issued by the on ramp provider
   532	 * @param dangerouslyOverrideOnRampEncryptionPublicKey *(optional)* Hex-encoded
   533	 *              uncompressed P-256 public key to encrypt to (use only in
   534	 *              tests/dev environment).  Defaults to the production on ramp encryption public key.
   535	 * @returns {Promise<string>} A base58check encoded borsh serialized envelope with the encrypted secret
   536	 *                            meant to be passed to the CreateFiatOnRampCredential activity
   537	 */
   538	export const encryptOnRampSecret = (
   539	  secret: string,
   540	  dangerouslyOverrideOnRampEncryptionPublicKey?: string,
   541	): string => {
   542	  return bs58check.encode(
   543	    hpkeEncrypt({
   544	      plainTextBuf: new TextEncoder().encode(secret),
   545	      targetKeyBuf: uncompressRawPublicKey(
   546	        uint8ArrayFromHexString(
   547	          dangerouslyOverrideOnRampEncryptionPublicKey ??
   548	            PRODUCTION_ON_RAMP_CREDENTIALS_ENCRYPTION_PUBLIC_KEY,
   549	        ),
   550	      ),
   551	    }),
   552	  );
   553	};
